Simple IPA passes have just one execute\n   196→   hook.  */\n   197→class simple_ipa_opt_pass : public opt_pass\n   198→{\n   199→protected:\n   200→  simple_ipa_opt_pass (const pass_data& data, gcc::context *ctxt)\n   201→    : opt_pass (data, ctxt)\n   202→  {\n   203→  }\n   204→};\n   205→\n   206→/* Pass properties.  */\n   207→#define PROP_gimple_any\t\t(1 << 0)\t/* entire gimple grammar */\n   208→#define PROP_gimple_lcf\t\t(1 << 1)\t/* lowered control flow */\n   209→#define PROP_gimple_leh\t\t(1 << 2)\t/* lowered eh */\n   210→#define PROP_cfg\t\t(1 << 3)\n   211→#define PROP_objsz\t\t(1 << 4)\t/* object sizes computed */\n   212→#define PROP_ssa\t\t(1 << 5)\n   213→#define PROP_no_crit_edges      (1 << 6)\n   214→#define PROP_rtl\t\t(1 << 7)\n   215→#define PROP_gimple_lomp\t(1 << 8)\t/* lowered OpenMP directives */\n   216→#define PROP_cfglayout\t \t(1 << 9)\t/* cfglayout mode on RTL */\n   217→#define PROP_gimple_lcx\t\t(1 << 10)       /* lowered complex */\n   218→#define PROP_loops\t\t(1 << 11)\t/* preserve loop structures */\n   219→#define PROP_gimple_lvec\t(1 << 12)       /* lowered vector */\n   220→#define PROP_gimple_eomp\t(1 << 13)       /* no OpenMP directives */\n   221→#define PROP_gimple_lva\t\t(1 << 14)       /* No va_arg internal function.  */\n   222→#define PROP_gimple_opt_math\t(1 << 15)\t/* Disable canonicalization\n   223→\t\t\t\t\t\t   of math functions; the\n   224→\t\t\t\t\t\t   current choices have\n   225→\t\t\t\t\t\t   been optimized.  */\n   226→#define PROP_gimple_lomp_dev\t(1 << 16)\t/* done omp_device_lower */\n   227→#define PROP_rtl_split_insns\t(1 << 17)\t/* RTL has insns split.  */\n   228→#define PROP_loop_opts_done\t(1 << 18)\t/* SSA loop optimizations\n   229→\t\t\t\t\t\t   have completed.  */\n   230→#define PROP_assumptions_done\t(1 << 19)\t/* Assume function kept\n   231→\t\t\t\t\t\t   around.  */\n   232→#define PROP_gimple_lbitint\t(1 << 20)       /* lowered large _BitInt */\n   233→#define PROP_last_full_fold\t(1 << 21)\t/* Start of last forwprop.  */\n   234→\n   235→#define PROP_gimple \\\n   236→  (PROP_gimple_any | PROP_gimple_lcf | PROP_gimple_leh | PROP_gimple_lomp)\n   237→\n   238→/* To-do flags.  */\n   239→/* Note (1ul << 31) is reserved for TODO_verify_il. */\n   240→#define TODO_do_not_ggc_collect\t\t(1 << 1)\n   241→#define TODO_cleanup_cfg        \t(1 << 5)\n   242→#define TODO_dump_symtab\t\t(1 << 7)\n   243→#define TODO_remove_functions\t\t(1 << 8)\n   244→\n   245→/* To-do flags for calls to update_ssa.  */\n   246→\n   247→/* Update the SSA form inserting PHI nodes for newly exposed symbols\n   248→   and virtual names marked for updating.  When updating real names,\n   249→   only insert PHI nodes for a real name O_j in blocks reached by all\n   250→   the new and old definitions for O_j.  If the iterated dominance\n   251→   frontier for O_j is not pruned, we may end up inserting PHI nodes\n   252→   in blocks that have one or more edges with no incoming definition\n   253→   for O_j.  This would lead to uninitialized warnings for O_j's\n   254→   symbol.  */\n   255→#define TODO_update_ssa\t\t\t(1 << 11)\n   256→\n   257→/* Update the SSA form without inserting any new PHI nodes at all.\n   258→   This is used by passes that have either inserted all the PHI nodes\n   259→   themselves or passes that need only to patch use-def and def-def\n   260→   chains for virtuals (e.g., DCE).  */\n   261→#define TODO_update_ssa_no_phi\t\t(1 << 12)\n   262→\n   263→/* Insert PHI nodes everywhere they are needed.  No pruning of the\n   264→   IDF is done.  This is used by passes that need the PHI nodes for\n   265→   O_j even if it means that some arguments will come from the default\n   266→   definition of O_j's symbol.\n   267→\n   268→   WARNING: If you need to use this flag, chances are that your pass\n   269→   may be doing something wrong.  Inserting PHI nodes for an old name\n   270→   where not all edges carry a new replacement may lead to silent\n   271→   codegen errors or spurious uninitialized warnings.  */\n   272→#define TODO_update_ssa_full_phi\t(1 << 13)\n   273→\n   274→/* Passes that update the SSA form on their own may want to delegate\n   275→   the updating of virtual names to the generic updater.  Since FUD\n   276→   chains are easier to maintain, this simplifies the work they need\n   277→   to do.  NOTE: If this flag is used, any OLD->NEW mappings for real\n   278→   names are explicitly destroyed and only the symbols marked for\n   279→   renaming are processed.  */\n   280→#define TODO_update_ssa_only_virtuals\t(1 << 14)\n   281→\n   282→/* Some passes leave unused local variables that can be removed from\n   283→   cfun->local_decls.  This reduces the size of dump files\n   284→   and the memory footprint for VAR_DECLs.  */\n   285→#define TODO_remove_unused_locals\t(1 << 15)\n   286→\n   287→/* Call df_finish at the end of the pass.  This is done after all of\n   288→   the dumpers have been allowed to run so that they have access to\n   289→   the instance before it is destroyed.  */\n   290→#define TODO_df_finish                  (1 << 17)\n   291→\n   292→/* Call df_verify at the end of the pass if checking is enabled.  */\n   293→#define TODO_df_verify                  (1 << 18)\n   294→\n   295→/* Internally used for the first instance of a pass.  */\n   296→#define TODO_mark_first_instance\t(1 << 19)\n   297→\n   298→/* Rebuild aliasing info.  */\n   299→#define TODO_rebuild_alias              (1 << 20)\n   300→\n   301→/* Rebuild the addressable-vars bitmap and do register promotion.  */\n   302→#define TODO_update_address_taken\t(1 << 21)\n   303→\n   304→/* Rebuild the callgraph edges.  */\n   305→#define TODO_rebuild_cgraph_edges       (1 << 22)\n   306→\n   307→/* Release function body (unless assumption function)\n   308→   and stop pass manager.  */\n   309→#define TODO_discard_function\t\t(1 << 23)\n   310→\n   311→/* (1ul << 31) is reserved for TODO_verify_il. */\n   312→\n   313→/* Internally used in execute_function_todo().  */\n   314→#define TODO_update_ssa_any\t\t\\\n   315→    (TODO_update_ssa\t\t\t\\\n   316→     | TODO_update_ssa_no_phi\t\t\\\n   317→     | TODO_update_ssa_full_phi\t\t\\\n   318→     | TODO_update_ssa_only_virtuals)\n   319→\n   320→/* To-do flags for pending_TODOs.  */\n   321→\n   322→/* Tell the next scalar cleanup pass that there is\n   323→   work for it to do.  */\n   324→#define PENDING_TODO_force_next_scalar_cleanup  (1 << 1)\n   325→\n   326→/* Register pass info. */\n   327→\n   328→enum pass_positioning_ops\n   329→{\n   330→  PASS_POS_INSERT_AFTER,  /* Insert after the reference pass.  */\n   331→  PASS_POS_INSERT_BEFORE, /* Insert before the reference pass.  */\n   332→  PASS_POS_REPLACE        /* Replace the reference pass.  */\n   333→};\n   334→\n   335→struct register_pass_info\n   336→{\n   337→  opt_pass *pass;\t\t    /* New pass to register.  */\n   338→  const char *reference_pass_name;  /* Name of the reference pass for hooking\n   339→                                       up the new pass.  */\n   340→  int ref_pass_instance_number;     /* Insert the pass at the specified\n   341→                                       instance number of the reference pass.\n   342→                                       Do it for every instance if it is 0.  */\n   343→  enum pass_positioning_ops pos_op; /* how to insert the new pass.  */\n   344→};\n   345→\n   346→/* Registers a new pass.  Either fill out the register_pass_info or specify\n   347→   the individual parameters.  The pass object is expected to have been\n   348→   allocated using operator new and the pass manager takes the ownership of\n   349→   the pass object.  */\n   350→extern void register_pass (register_pass_info *);\n   351→extern void register_pass (opt_pass* pass, pass_positioning_ops pos,\n   352→\t\t\t   const char* ref_pass_name, int ref_pass_inst_number);\n   353→\n   354→extern When updating real names,\n   only insert PHI nodes for a real name O_j in blocks reached by all\n   the new and old definitions for O_j.  If the iterated dominance\n   frontier for O_j is not pruned, we may end up inserting PHI nodes\n   in blocks that have one or more edges with no incoming definition\n   for O_j.  This would lead to uninitialized warnings for O_j's\n   symbol.  */\n#define TODO_update_ssa\t\t\t(1 << 11)\n\n/* Update the SSA form without inserting any new PHI nodes at all.\n   This is used by passes that have either inserted all the PHI nodes\n   themselves or passes that need only to patch use-def and def-def\n   chains for virtuals (e.g., DCE).  */\n#define TODO_update_ssa_no_phi\t\t(1 << 12)\n\n/* Insert PHI nodes everywhere they are needed.  No pruning of the\n   IDF is done.  This is used by passes that need the PHI nodes for\n   O_j even if it means that some arguments will come from the default\n   definition of O_j's symbol.\n\n   WARNING: If you need to use this flag, chances are that your pass\n   may be doing something wrong.  Inserting PHI nodes for an old name\n   where not all edges carry a new replacement may lead to silent\n   codegen errors or spurious uninitialized warnings.  */\n#define TODO_update_ssa_full_phi\t(1 << 13)\n\n/* Passes that update the SSA form on their own may want to delegate\n   the updating of virtual names to the generic updater.  Since FUD\n   chains are easier to maintain, this simplifies the work they need\n   to do.  NOTE: If this flag is used, any OLD->NEW mappings for real\n   names are explicitly destroyed and only the symbols marked for\n   renaming are processed.  */\n#define TODO_update_ssa_only_virtuals\t(1 << 14)\n\n/* Some passes leave unused local variables that can be removed from\n   cfun->local_decls.  This reduces the size of dump files\n   and the memory footprint for VAR_DECLs.  */\n#define TODO_remove_unused_locals\t(1 << 15)\n\n/* Call df_finish at the end of the pass.  This is done after all of\n   the dumpers have been allowed to run so that they have access to\n   the instance before it is destroyed.  */\n#define TODO_df_finish                  (1 << 17)\n\n/* Call df_verify at the end of the pass if checking is enabled.  */\n#define TODO_df_verify                  (1 << 18)\n\n/* Internally used for the first instance of a pass.  */\n#define TODO_mark_first_instance\t(1 << 19)\n\n/* Rebuild aliasing info.  */\n#define TODO_rebuild_alias              (1 << 20)\n\n/* Rebuild the addressable-vars bitmap and do register promotion.  */\n#define TODO_update_address_taken\t(1 << 21)\n\n/* Rebuild the callgraph edges.  */\n#define TODO_rebuild_cgraph_edges       (1 << 22)\n\n/* Release function body (unless assumption function)\n   and stop pass manager.  */\n#define TODO_discard_function\t\t(1 << 23)\n\n/* (1ul << 31) is reserved for TODO_verify_il. */\n\n/* Internally used in execute_function_todo().  */\n#define TODO_update_ssa_any\t\t\\\n    (TODO_update_ssa\t\t\t\\\n     | TODO_update_ssa_no_phi\t\t\\\n     | TODO_update_ssa_full_phi\t\t\\\n     | TODO_update_ssa_only_virtuals)\n\n/* To-do flags for pending_TODOs.  */\n\n/* Tell the next scalar cleanup pass that there is\n   work for it to do.  */\n#define PENDING_TODO_force_next_scalar_cleanup  (1 << 1)\n\n/* Register pass info. */\n\nenum pass_positioning_ops\n{\n  PASS_POS_INSERT_AFTER,  /* Insert after the reference pass.  */\n  PASS_POS_INSERT_BEFORE, /* Insert before the reference pass.  */\n  PASS_POS_REPLACE        /* Replace the reference pass.  */\n};\n\nstruct register_pass_info\n{\n  opt_pass *pass;\t\t    /* New pass to register.  */\n  const char *reference_pass_name;  /* Name of the reference pass for hooking\n                                       up the new pass.  */\n  int ref_pass_instance_number;     /* Insert the pass at the specified\n                                       instance number of the reference pass.\n                                       Do it for every instance if it is 0.  */\n  enum pass_positioning_ops pos_op; /* how to insert the new pass.  */\n};\n\n/* Registers a new pass.  Either fill out the register_pass_info or specify\n   the individual parameters.  The pass object is expected to have been\n   allocated using operator new and the pass manager takes the ownership of\n   the pass object.  */\nextern void register_pass (register_pass_info *);\nextern void register_pass (opt_pass* pass, pass_positioning_ops pos,\n\t\t\t   const char* ref_pass_name, int ref_pass_inst_number);\n\nextern gimple_opt_pass *make_pass_asan (gcc::context 1 : 0);\n  if (TREE_CODE (arg) != ADDR_EXPR)\n    return false;\n  arg = TREE_OPERAND (arg, 0);\n  if (TREE_CODE (arg) != FUNCTION_DECL)\n    return false;\n  int flags = flags_from_decl_or_type (arg);\n\n  /* If the function is noreturn then it cannot be removed. */\n  if (flags & ECF_NORETURN)\n    return false;\n\n  /* The function needs to be const or pure and non looping.  */\n  return (flags & (ECF_CONST|ECF_PURE))\n\t  && !(flags & ECF_LOOPING_CONST_OR_PURE);\n}\n\n/* If STMT is not already marked necessary, mark it, and add it to the\n   worklist if ADD_TO_WORKLIST is true.  */\n\nstatic inline void\nmark_stmt_necessary (gimple *stmt, bool add_to_worklist)\n{\n  gcc_assert (stmt);\n\n  if (gimple_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY))\n    return;\n\n  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n    {\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"Marking useful stmt: \");\n      print_gimple_stmt (dump_file, stmt, 0, TDF_SLIM);\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"\\n\");\n    }\n\n  gimple_set_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY, true);\n  if (add_to_worklist)\n    worklist.safe_push (stmt);\n  if (add_to_worklist && bb_contains_live_stmts && !is_gimple_debug (stmt))\n    bitmap_set_bit (bb_contains_live_stmts, gimple_bb (stmt)->index);","numLines":200,"startLine":1,"totalLines":2258}}}

\"GCC's optimization pass registration and execution follows a hierarchical chain:\\n\\n**1. Pass Definition (gcc/passes.def)**: The master list of all optimization passes is defined in gcc/passes.def using macro-based declarations. The file uses INSERT_PASSES_AFTER to define pass groups (all_lowering_passes, all_small_ipa_passes, all_regular_ipa_passes, all_late_ipa_passes, all_passes), NEXT_PASS to register individual passes in order, and PUSH_INSERT_PASSES_WITHIN/POP_INSERT_PASSES to define nested pass groups. This file is processed by gen-pass-instances.awk to generate pass-instances.def.\\n\\n**2. Pass Manager Interface (gcc/pass_manager.h)**: The pass_manager class in gcc/pass_manager.h orchestrates pass execution. It contains references to all registered passes (e.g., m_pass_build_cfg_1, m_pass_dce_1) that are generated via macro expansion of pass-instances.def. The class maintains pass_lists arrays indexed by enum pass_list values, manages pass registration, and provides methods like execute_early_local_passes() and execute_pass_mode_switching().\\n\\n**3. Pass Manager Implementation (gcc/passes.cc)**: The gcc/passes.cc file implements the pass_manager constructor, which instantiates all passes by calling their make_pass_* factory functions. It also implements the core execution functions: execute_pass_list (recursively executes all passes in a list) and execute_one_pass (executes a single pass while managing gates, TODOs, and pass properties). The variable current_pass tracks the currently executing pass for debugging.\\n\\n**4. Pass Infrastructure (gcc/tree-pass.h)**: This header defines the core pass infrastructure: the opt_pass base class with virtual methods (gate, execute, clone, set_pass_param), struct pass_data (containing pass metadata like type, name, and property requirements), and derived classes gimple_opt_pass, rtl_opt_pass, simple_ipa_opt_pass, and ipa_opt_pass_d. The file also declares all make_pass_* factory functions (e.g., make_pass_dce, make_pass_cd_dce) and the register_pass infrastructure for plugin passes.\\n\\n**5. Concrete Example - Dead Code Elimination (gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc)**: The tree-ssa-dce.cc file implements a concrete GIMPLE optimization pass. It defines pass_data_dce as a constant struct with GIMPLE_PASS type and required properties (PROP_cfg | PROP_ssa). The pass_dce_base class extends gimple_opt_pass and implements gate() to check flag_tree_dce and set_pass_param() for configuration. The pass_dce class overrides execute() to call execute_dce with aggressive=false, while pass_cd_dce uses aggressive=(optimize >= 2). The make_pass_dce factory function creates and returns new pass_dce instances.\\n\\n**Execution Chain**: When compilation begins, pass_manager instantiates all passes. The compiler then calls execute_pass_list on the root pass, which recursively traverses the pass tree. For each pass, execute_one_pass checks the gate predicate, calls execute(), applies TODO flags, and recursively executes sub-passes if the gate succeeds. This ensures passes execute in the correct order with proper dependency management.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":216,"cache_read_input_tokens":59322,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":216},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7f2c3fa8-758a-409d-8691-cb759adeb2c6","uuid":"da8903cf-2297-43ae-9692-4ace5d16c07b"}

The file uses INSERT_PASSES_AFTER to define pass groups (all_lowering_passes, all_small_ipa_passes, all_regular_ipa_passes, all_late_ipa_passes, all_passes), NEXT_PASS to register individual passes in order, and PUSH_INSERT_PASSES_WITHIN/POP_INSERT_PASSES to define nested pass groups. This file is processed by gen-pass-instances.awk to generate pass-instances.def.\\n\\n**2. Pass Manager Interface (gcc/pass_manager.h)**: The pass_manager class in gcc/pass_manager.h orchestrates pass execution. It contains references to all registered passes (e.g., m_pass_build_cfg_1, m_pass_dce_1) that are generated via macro expansion of pass-instances.def. The class maintains pass_lists arrays indexed by enum pass_list values, manages pass registration, and provides methods like execute_early_local_passes() and execute_pass_mode_switching().\\n\\n**3. Pass Manager Implementation (gcc/passes.cc)**: The gcc/passes.cc file implements the pass_manager constructor, which instantiates all passes by calling their make_pass_* factory functions. It also implements the core execution functions: execute_pass_list (recursively executes all passes in a list) and execute_one_pass (executes a single pass while managing gates, TODOs, and pass properties). The variable current_pass tracks the currently executing pass for debugging.\\n\\n**4. Pass Infrastructure (gcc/tree-pass.h)**: This header defines the core pass infrastructure: the opt_pass base class with virtual methods (gate, execute, clone, set_pass_param), struct pass_data (containing pass metadata like type, name, and property requirements), and derived classes gimple_opt_pass, rtl_opt_pass, simple_ipa_opt_pass, and ipa_opt_pass_d. The file also declares all make_pass_* factory functions (e.g., make_pass_dce, make_pass_cd_dce) and the register_pass infrastructure for plugin passes.\\n\\n**5. Concrete Example - Dead Code Elimination (gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc)**: The tree-ssa-dce.cc file implements a concrete GIMPLE optimization pass. It defines pass_data_dce as a constant struct with GIMPLE_PASS type and required properties (PROP_cfg | PROP_ssa). The pass_dce_base class extends gimple_opt_pass and implements gate() to check flag_tree_dce and set_pass_param() for configuration. The pass_dce class overrides execute() to call execute_dce with aggressive=false, while pass_cd_dce uses aggressive=(optimize >= 2). The make_pass_dce factory function creates and returns new pass_dce instances.\\n\\n**Execution Chain**: When compilation begins, pass_manager instantiates all passes. The compiler then calls execute_pass_list on the root pass, which recursively traverses the pass tree. For each pass, execute_one_pass checks the gate predicate, calls execute(), applies TODO flags, and recursively executes sub-passes if the gate succeeds. This ensures passes execute in the correct order with proper dependency management.\"\n   129→}\n   130→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
